1180、I <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/used">used</a> to think the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/worst">worst</a> thing in life was to end up all alone. It's not. The <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/worst">worst</a> thing in life is to end up with people that make you feel all alone.   我曾以为人生最糟糕的是孤独终老，其实不是，最糟糕的是与让你倍感孤独的人一起终老。(罗宾·威廉姆斯)<br/>
1181、If all the world <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/hated">hated</a> you, and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/believed">believed</a> you <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/wicked">wicked</a>, while your own <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/conscience">conscience</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/approved">approved</a> you, and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/absolved">absolved</a> you from <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/guilt">guilt</a>, you would not be without friends.   哪怕全世界的人都恨你，认为你坏，只要你自问无愧，你不会没朋友。《简爱》<br/>
1182、Don't <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/forget">forget</a> the things you once <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/owned">owned</a>. <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Treasure">Treasure</a> the things you can't get. Don't give up the things that <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/belong">belong</a> to you and keep those <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/lost">lost</a> things in <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/memory">memory</a>.   曾经拥有的，不要忘记。不能得到的，更要珍惜。属于自己的，不要放弃。已经失去的，留作回忆。《曾经》<br/>
1183、<a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Anyone">Anyone</a> who <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/stops">stops</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/learning">learning</a> is old, <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/whether">whether</a> at <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/twenty">twenty</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/eighty">eighty</a>. <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Anyone">Anyone</a> who <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/keeps">keeps</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/learning">learning</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/stays">stays</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/young">young</a>. The greatest thing in life is to keep your mind <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/young">young</a>.   任何停止学习的人都已经老了，无论是20岁还是80岁。坚持学习的人永远年轻，人生最美好的事就是保持年轻的心。<br/>
1184、This is a big and beautiful world. Most of us live and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/die">die</a> in the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/same">same</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/corner">corner</a> where we were <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/born">born</a> and never get to see any of it. I don't want to be most of us.   这个世界如此辽阔和美丽，而大多数人从生到死，都在同一个角落里不挪窝，没见识过别处的风景，我不想成为那种人。《权力的游戏》<br/>
1185、<a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Knowing">Knowing</a> after all the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/unreturned">unreturned</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/phone">phone</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/calls">calls</a>, broken-hearts, through the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/blunders">blunders</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/misread">misread</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/signals">signals</a>, through all the pain and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/embarrassment">embarrassment</a> you never <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/gave">gave</a> up hope.   经历无数次伤心、自作多情，和数不清的痛苦尴尬后，你依然相信真爱。《他没那么喜欢你》<br/>
1186、Don't be <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/jealous">jealous</a> that people have <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/done">done</a> better than you. All you need to do is to keep <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/breaking">breaking</a> your own <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/record">record</a> every day, for success is a <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/fight">fight</a> between you and yourself.   不要羡慕别人做得比你好，只需要每天打破自己的记录，因为成功是你和自己打仗。<br/>
1187、Being <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/simple">simple</a> is not <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/settling">settling</a> for <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/less">less</a>, it is being <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/satisfied">satisfied</a> with <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/having">having</a> just enough. <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Having">Having</a> enough is not <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/longing">longing</a> for more, it is being <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/content">content</a> with <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/having">having</a> you by my side.   简约不是少，而是没有多余。足够也不是多，而是刚好你在。<br/>
1188、<a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Calling">Calling</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/somebody">somebody</a> else <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/fat">fat</a> won't make you any <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/skinnier">skinnier</a>. <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/Calling">Calling</a> someone <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/stupid">stupid</a> doesn't make you any <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/smarter">smarter</a>. All you can do in life is try to <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/solve">solve</a> the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/problem">problem</a> in <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/front">front</a> of you.   笑别人胖不能让自己瘦，说别人傻不能让自己聪明。你的人生就是解决自己面临的问题。《贱女孩》<br/>
1189、Sometimes you're <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/flush">flush</a> and sometimes you're <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/bust">bust</a>, and when you're up, it's never as good as it <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/seems">seems</a>, and when you're down, you never think you'll be up again, but life <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/goes">goes</a> on.   人生有起有落。起时，你不会在意；落时，你以为爬不起。但生命仍要继续。《美国毒枭》<br/>
